  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d5acfbb4-6f43-4f14-96d4-c2d6f0288ce4'
      });

  <span id="freeText9721884756180632521" style="display:none"><b>What happens when in order to win, you’re forced to lose?</b><br /><br />The only daughter of an infamous Las Vegas pimp, Raven Morretti grew up an outsider. Liberated from the neglectful home of her prostitute mother, she finds solace as a mechanic. With few friends, she’s content with the simple life. Flying under the radar is all she knows, and more than she expects.<br /><br /><b>Until she catches the eye of local celebrity, UFL playboy Jonah Slade. </b><br /><br />Weeks away from his title fight, Jonah is determined to stay focused on everything he’s trained so hard to achieve. Undefeated in the octagon, he’s at the height of his career. But resisting Raven’s effortless allure and uncomplicated nature is a fight he can’t win. <br /><br />Jonah trades in his bad-boy reputation and puts his heart on the line. But when her father contacts her, setting in motion the ugly truth of her destiny, Jonah must choose. In a high-stakes gamble where love and freedom hang in the balance, a war is waged where the price of losing is a fate worse than death.<br /><br /><b>Will the hotheaded Jonah be able to restrain his inner fighter to save the woman he loves? </b><br /><br /><b>Or will Raven be forced into a life she’s been desperate to avoid?</b><br /><br /><b>Word Count: 112,406 </b></span>

  <span id="freeText5611256731984668239" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW<b> -mature content reader discretion is advised.</b><br>3.5 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br><br><b>First and foremost I want to start by saying that Jonah can get me on any of the following days </b><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/tumblr_mhjn0p7uOX1s4ez6ko1_500_zpsec127843.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><b>My Casting </b><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/Final%20edited%20version%20pt2/meganfox3_zps9cd80ec7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411577i/808722.jpg" alt=" photo 165d3203-c94a-4626-9b34-378dbcb2aaf7_zps0be9860f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>I read the beginning of this book in Horror</b><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/shockedgif1_zpsf83ff381.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411577ra/808723.gif" alt=" photo shockedgif1_zpsf83ff381.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Thinking who could EVER do such a thing. Horror was quickly replaced with</b><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/tumblr_m4h3v17B5i1rwcc6bo1_400_zpsbdfdde5d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><br><b>The transgressions of our mothers may haunt us...</b><br>When the book begins we are transported 21 years into the past, we learn of the transgressions a mother makes the day her daughter is born.<br>And the price the child must pay once she reaches legal age. Prostitution. Birthed with the innocence of a babe yet bred to leave her virtue behind for a life her mother knows well.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/99d9a520-ceb6-4d88-ae29-020b51ae8566_zps7ddeb6b4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/73279227-c033-4d81-afbe-edf5192d0ee5_zps121c1ccb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/4f08df3c-36c8-45f1-a0a3-d1d791975dc2_zps1af24f40.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411577i/808726.jpg" alt=" photo 4f08df3c-36c8-45f1-a0a3-d1d791975dc2_zps1af24f40.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Raven</b><br>20 years later Raven has been estranged from her mother for over 2 years and from her father her whole life. She works as a mechanic and resides above the shop. Guy was her high school shop teacher he taught her about cars and saw she had talent. He is now her boss and is the only other person she is close to besides her best friend Eve. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411577ra/808727.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mj8is5NMl51qffcrao5_500_zps6e2b1303.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411577ra/808728.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mj8is5NMl51qffcrao3_500_zps3ed4e9e7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411577ra/808729.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mj8is5NMl51qffcrao1_500_zpsafabd0ee.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jonah</b><br>Jonah "The Assassin" Slade is a MMA fighter. He is currently undefeated and known for being a "Ladies Man" <br><br><b>
  <i>'I do not hit the same honey pot twice.'</i>
</b><br><br> Yup, he has a rep and it's not just for kicking ass in the octagon. *wink, wink*<br>Jonah is looking to fix up his '61 Chevy, Impala and Guy refers "Ray" aka Raven for the job. When they meet she's instantly starstruck and slowly gathers herself. She takes the job and goes fan-girl crazy, on the inside of course!<br><br><i>
  <b>'I’m going to be fixing up a car with Jonah “The Assassin” Slade. What have I gotten myself into?'</b>
</i> ~Raven<br><br>As you can imagine Jonah is taken aback not only because Ray turns out to <u>not</u> be male but a female. But A BEAUTIFUL female. It's her beauty, a beauty that drys out his mouth... Raising up a thirst for her in a way he realizes can only be quenched by tasting what she has to offer. <br><br>Friendship takes root fast between these two as does a relationship. Making the decision to leave the bachelor style life behind was not a hard choice for Jonah. His feelings for Raven mad that one of the easiest choices he ever had to make.<br><br><b>
  <i>'So this is love. My life will never be the same.'</i>
</b> ~Jonah<br><br><br>Things get serious and Raven knows she must tell him the truth about who she is. Scared...she is scared he'll want nothing to do with her once he knows her parentage. What she does not know is that he has already made up his mine about her.<br><br> <i>
  <b>"I want <u>you</u>. And that includes everything that makes you who you are.”</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><i>
  <u>
    <b>'But he was no savior. He was my undertaker.'</b>
  </u>
</i> ~Milena<br><br><b> *Whispers* Daddy... Or Predator</b><br>Love life and automobiles; that was Raven's life until her phone rings and changes everything. Her father wants to meet with her and because of the little girl inside who holds out on hope she accepts the invitation. <br><br>When daddy puts on his pimp hat and drops the bomb that Raven will be his property on her 21st birthday she's utterly devastated. That little slice of hope is now crushed into tiny pieces of sorrow.<br><br><i>
  <b>'The life I’d built for myself, friends, Jonah, all of it was erased in less than an hour. I’m chained to the ugliness, caged in a nightmare with no chance of escape.'</b>
</i> ~Raven<br><br>And when she tells Jonah he goes <b>APE SHIT -I AM THE KING OF THE JUNGLE- C R A Z Y.</b><br><br><br>Can their love survive this? *Grins slowly* You have to read to find out! <br><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorites</u>
</b><br><br><u>
  <b>Fave Lines and/or thoughts unsaid</b>
</u><br><br><i>'Everything from my thoughts to my dick gravitates in her direction.'</i> ~Jonah<br><br><i>'I’ve known her for a week, and I’m spilling my guts about my dad like a pigtailed girl at a sleepover.'</i> ~Jonah<br><br><br><b>
  <u>Lines that made me SWOON</u>
</b><br><br><i>'I would give up anything for her, including my life’s dream. She’s my dream now.</i>' ~Jonah<br><br><i>“You’re part of me now. I’d do anything for you. I’ll fight for your life as I’d fight for my own.”</i> ~Jonah<br><br><i>“I’ll make it my life’s mission to make up for every second you were neglected.”</i> ~Jonah<br><br><br><u>
  <b>Lines that made me laugh out loud</b>
</u><br><br><i>“That’s it!”</i> Locking her wide eyes with mine, she throws her hands in the air. <i>“I’m done. I’m switching teams. I despise men and from now on will only date women.”</i><br><br><i>“Raven, a little later we can play Titanic,”</i> he calls over his shoulder.<i> “I’ll yell ice burg and you can go down.”</i> ~Blake<br><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>Did I enjoy this book?<b> HELL TO THE YES!!</b> I loved it actually.<br>So why 3 stars? I really really <b>
  <u>really</u>
</b> wanted to give this book that 4th star but I couldn't. And here is why. The whole insta-love storyline. Ummm yeah, I just can't work with that. It's cool for people who like that, I just ain't one of them. Then he barely knew her but let her move in pretty quickly. I wasn't buying that one either.<br><br>So, besides those two things this book ROCKED for me. It was filled with some very<i>
  <b> sexy-give-it-to-me-baby</b>
</i> scenes and I'm not referring to just Jonah. Raven's sex appeal burnt up the pages just as much as Jonah's. Yup I was turned on by a chick. What the hell is going on? Has this happened to anyone else while reading? Maybe not this book but another? I need to know I'm not alone. <br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Lovable<br>Writing Style- Good<br>Plot/Storyline- Good<br>Steam Factor- High/ Extremely HOT<br>Overall- I loved it!!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17828234001299290642"><b>5 ☆s</b><br/>Wow, Just.. WOW!! This book is something else only! Freakin' fabulous!<br/><br/><b>It left me totally dazed and high!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403987ra/786017.gif' width='320' height='220' alt='dazed' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My casting..<br/><u>Jonah</u><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808475._SY540_.jpg' width='340' height='480' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><u>Raven</u><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808476.png' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><u>Dominique</u><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808477._SY540_.jpg' width='360' height='420' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>He's the local star, A fighter.. feral, A ripped sexy hunk, A local casanova..<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808478._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>She's the daughter of Las Vagas' infamous pimp, A mechanic..<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808479.jpg' width='320' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>They meet, sparks fly..<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808480._SX540_.jpg' width='280' height='180' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>They fall in love, He's the only one who's ever cared to help her, the only one who's ever known her worth, the only one who's every loved her.<br/>NOW<br/>the Beast wants her, to own her, to sell her.. She'</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17828234001299290642" style="display:none"><b>5 ☆s</b><br>Wow, Just.. WOW!! This book is something else only! Freakin' fabulous!<br><br><b>It left me totally dazed and high!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403987ra/786017.gif" width="320" height="220" alt="dazed" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My casting..<br><u>Jonah</u><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808475._SY540_.jpg" width="340" height="480" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><u>Raven</u><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808476.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><u>Dominique</u><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808477._SY540_.jpg" width="360" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>He's the local star, A fighter.. feral, A ripped sexy hunk, A local casanova..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808478._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>She's the daughter of Las Vagas' infamous pimp, A mechanic..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808479.jpg" width="320" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They meet, sparks fly..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808480._SX540_.jpg" width="280" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They fall in love, He's the only one who's ever cared to help her, the only one who's ever known her worth, the only one who's every loved her.<br>NOW<br>the Beast wants her, to own her, to sell her.. She's in danger and only her Prince Charming can save her, He's the only one who can help her.<br><br>This book is like a role-reversal, Beauty and the Beast. Here the Beast is the father, The Pimp and Prince Charming is UFL playboy Jonah Slade.<br><br>He'll do it all.. fight for his love, break down all the doors in between them.. He'll protect her, save the day and win his love. ;)</i></b><br><br>This book is beautiful and the dual pov is just a wonderful treat.<br>The Author, Jamie Salsbury has written this book is such a compelling way, it draws you in and captures your mind.<br><br>I finished this book in 1 sitting and the whole day after that, only Raven and Jonah's story was playing in my head.<br>Its very unique the story line, the plot might be a little read before but still the way it is portrayed.. Its beautiful, just like the magnificent cover of this novel.<br><br>All the characters had such a strong value in this book. I loved them all..<br><br><b>Jonah Slade, 'The Assassin'</b><br>He is wonderful, I wanted to hump him and cuddle him and then eat him up.. Such a strong powerful character.. Feral and headstrong, a fighter, a lover and an amazing person.<br><br><b>Raven Morretti, Ray..</b><br>Beautiful innocent naive girl, She possesses him, they compel each other and they fall madly in love..<br><br><i>“You’re like that single wild flower that grows from the crack in the pavement: miraculous growth with no water source or fertile soil. A person walking by would step around that flower to avoid crushing it. It’s not like the field of wild flowers you tromp through carelessly, crushing them under your feet, knowing that the next day will bring a hundred more.”</i><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808481.jpg" width="230" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The sex scenes were fire burning hot.. like you need to shower after them because they were more than sexy and sizzling, It was compelling, sensual, passionate and oozing chemistry<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411520ra/808482.gif" width="320" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411520i/808483.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411520ra/808484.gif" width="350" height="235" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411520ra/808485.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>This book is beautiful, amazing and just WOW and the +point is... <u>NO CLIFFHANGER!!</u></b> <i>*phew*</i><br><br><i>“Gives a whole new meaning to the term body shop.” His eyes settle on her legs. “Nice legs, what time do they open?”<br><br>“If I flip a coin, what are the chances I’ll get head?”<br><br>“Raven, a little later we can play Titanic,” he calls over his shoulder. “I’ll yell ice burg and you can go down.”<i> ---- <b>I LOVED Blake, Cannot wait for his book!! :D :D</b></i></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17828234001299290642" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/551333006?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer551333006" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17382740580117236880"><b>5 Fighting Stars!!!!! </b>  <br/><br/>Jonah is a bad ass MMA fighter in Vegas. Ever since his father died when he was twelve, he centered his world around fighting. He is on his way to be champion. He hangs out with his friends, trains, fights... he doesn’t do relationships.<br/><b>
  <i>Ah hell, I don’t even know her name.<br/>Oh well. Won’t be the first time I bang a nameless face.</i>
</b><br/>Yeah- we get that from the very beginning, but he’s honest about it.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/9a42a02b-f115-4a0e-80ff-eab3aca85879_zpsf51791a3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411935i/809792._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 9a42a02b-f115-4a0e-80ff-eab3aca85879_zpsf51791a3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/761303d0-4c7d-4530-bc2a-2f8efb49ddcf_zpsdd4287f8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411935i/809793.jpg' alt=' photo 761303d0-4c7d-4530-bc2a-2f8efb49ddcf_zpsdd4287f8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Raven Morretti lives a quite life. She is a mechanic in a garage, s</span>
  <span id="freeText17382740580117236880" style="display:none"><b>5 Fighting Stars!!!!! </b>  <br><br>Jonah is a bad ass MMA fighter in Vegas. Ever since his father died when he was twelve, he centered his world around fighting. He is on his way to be champion. He hangs out with his friends, trains, fights... he doesn’t do relationships.<br><b>
  <i>Ah hell, I don’t even know her name.<br>Oh well. Won’t be the first time I bang a nameless face.</i>
</b><br>Yeah- we get that from the very beginning, but he’s honest about it.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/9a42a02b-f115-4a0e-80ff-eab3aca85879_zpsf51791a3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411935i/809792._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9a42a02b-f115-4a0e-80ff-eab3aca85879_zpsf51791a3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/761303d0-4c7d-4530-bc2a-2f8efb49ddcf_zpsdd4287f8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411935i/809793.jpg" alt=" photo 761303d0-4c7d-4530-bc2a-2f8efb49ddcf_zpsdd4287f8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Raven Morretti lives a quite life. She is a mechanic in a garage, she has one close friend she is a bit shy and inexperienced. She comes from a crazy background. Her mother is a prostitute and her father is a famous pimp/criminal in Vegas. She is estranged from the both of them. She tries to make the best of her life. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/68e8f7c1-de15-4b12-86b1-6e05295af6ca_zpse1d29277.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411935i/809794.jpg" alt=" photo 68e8f7c1-de15-4b12-86b1-6e05295af6ca_zpse1d29277.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jonah needs a mechanic to help him fix up one of his classic cars, and that is how he and Raven meet. Jonah doesn’t understand the feelings he has for Raven. He never feels this way about women. He likes her, sees her more than just a conquest. He wants to take care of her. Protect her. <br><br><b>There is no working this girl out of my system.</b><br><br>They start spending more time together and are both falling for one another. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I want you. And that includes everything that makes you who you are.”</i>
</b><br><br>As things start to get more serious, Jonah is afraid of screwing things up. He knows he has a reputation, and Raven is so innocent. Love the advice his friend Owen gives...<br><br><b>
  <i>“What if I... I don’t know, screw things up?”<br>Owen’s eyebrows hit his hairline. “Dude, if practice makes perfect, you should have your PhD in sex. Pretty sure you won’t screw it up.”</i>
</b><br><br>When they do get together, sparks fly. These two have chemistry. Heat. Passion. <br><br><b>So this is love. My life will never be the same.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/bde7ebdb-fa70-470d-87ad-b3cf742b50e9_zps67e757a9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411935i/809795.jpg" alt=" photo bde7ebdb-fa70-470d-87ad-b3cf742b50e9_zps67e757a9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jonah and Raven have a beautiful relationship- I love them together. But then, her father comes into the picture and all hell breaks lose. They have to fight to stay together. Jonah has to figure out if he will be able to lose something big to win an even bigger prize than the title- Raven. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/afdb0fb2-0627-4486-aee5-c23adc9c01e8_zps50706d19.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411935i/809796.jpg" alt=" photo afdb0fb2-0627-4486-aee5-c23adc9c01e8_zps50706d19.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh my wow! I was so pleasantly surprised by how much I loved this book! Jonah- this guy was as close to Travis Maddox as I have found, and I love me some Travis! Couldn’t get enough of Jonah. He was loving, kind, protective, and of course tattooed and sexy. Raven and Jonah didn’t have a lot of drama or angst between them which was great... just a lot of stuff from the outside. And I absolutely LOVED Blake! I cannot wait to read the next book in the series about him- he had so many great lines! What a funny and loyal guy! If you haven’t read this book- you need to!!! This one is a must read!!! <br><br><b>“You’re mine baby. Always.”</b></span>

<div id="review_547850128" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547850128" />
    <a title="Shelley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7526630-shelley"><img alt="Shelley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370799427p2/7526630.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/547850128?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelley" href="/user/show/7526630-shelley">Shelley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7526630-shelley?shelf=uber-alpha-male">uber-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7526630-shelley?shelf=no-just-no">no-just-no</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7526630-shelley?shelf=drama-drama-drama">drama-drama-drama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547850128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11994591103561898177"><b>With such a gorgeous sensual cover, the irresistible temptation of an MMA bad boy; the idea that the heroine might be a strong -take- no- bullshit- character by suggesting her job as a mechanic and the fact that she hales from the Vegas underworld. I was immediately seduced into downloading a sample.</b><br/> <br/>The writing…oh joy! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411415ra/807987.gif' alt=' photo 2pac_facepalm_gif.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It’s written in the first person present tense and it’s horrible. <br/>I hate this format, it screams amateur to me. This is where I should have left it alone and just walked away. <br/>Th</span>
  <span id="freeText11994591103561898177" style="display:none"><b>With such a gorgeous sensual cover, the irresistible temptation of an MMA bad boy; the idea that the heroine might be a strong -take- no- bullshit- character by suggesting her job as a mechanic and the fact that she hales from the Vegas underworld. I was immediately seduced into downloading a sample.</b><br> <br>The writing…oh joy! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411415ra/807987.gif" alt=" photo 2pac_facepalm_gif.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It’s written in the first person present tense and it’s horrible. <br>I hate this format, it screams amateur to me. This is where I should have left it alone and just walked away. <br>That being said I have endured this style in the past and if it is done subtly, with elegance and is pivotal to the telling, I can cope. So against my better judgement I cave and click buy as I am still seduced by the premise of this story.<br><br>Stupid, stupid me!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411415ra/807988.gif" alt=" photo gibbsheadslap_zps630a6258.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The over use of <b> I </b> and <b> my</b> has the same result as nails on a chalk board, but I grind my teeth and persevere with the plot and what I think will be a strong feisty heroine and a mean sexy bad-boy in need of a hammer wielding mechanic to break through his defences. <br><br>How wrong could I have been? What follows is a whole lot of insta; insta-attraction, insta-lust, insta-love and insta-bility. There is no relationship development, just a whole lot of possessive animalistic growling from Jonah and blushing from Raven. Ridiculous, especially when this is supposed to be for a mature paying audience. I expect more than that I’m afraid.<br><br>It is quickly established that Raven is not the kick-ass-strong-willed heroine I had assumed. She is a twenty year old <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[virgin <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> girl (not a woman!)Who behaves like a 12 year old, she sobs and cry’s over everything!<br> <br>Seriously …EVERYTHING! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411415ra/807989.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lv1s5cvcUM1qcqhq7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is such a constant emotion for her that it garners nothing but my irritation. She blushes like a bloody teenager over one look from Jonah and giggles over the most ridiculous jokes. Her character in relation to her upbringing is just totally implausible to me.<br><br>Jonah is supposed to be this hard as ice bachelor who never sleeps with the same woman twice. So having slept with scores of woman I do not expect this experienced man to behave like a teenager at the sight of a lacy bra! Sure, he’s met the woman of his dreams but his insta-capitulation is incredulous. He growls as much as Raven sobs which only leaves me feeling...well, incredulous (again!).<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411415ra/807990.gif" alt=" photo woman_wtf_gif_zps69572115.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The plot is predictable and its effortless staying steps ahead of these characters and the evolving scheme. Such a pity our MC’s are too tragic to see it. <br><br>This has no angst but lots of drama of which I couldn't really give a toss about, especially when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the MC’s decide to just accept the situation and not find any other alternative, ultimately trusting a renowned criminal to honour his word. As if! Talk about ignorance.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This has some sweet moments between Raven and Jonah and her upbringing is a harsh one. The authors attempt at creating an empathy with Raven is justifiable, but it does not make up for her other shortcomings. <br><br>I predict this will be a hit with the ‘Indie’ readers who don’t mind this structure and are able to suspend disbelief, overlook some editing issues, and prefer reading just for the eye candy that is Jonah and Raven. <br><br>Me? I am not impressed.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11994591103561898177" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer551233593" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3901465538664650649"><b>4 FIGHTING and FLYING Stars<br/><br/><i>Nothing, not even destiny, could keep me from you.</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411920ra/809736.gif' width='500' height='233' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>What does a mechanic...</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411920i/809737.png' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>and a fighter have in common?</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411920ra/809738.gif' width='300' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>EVERYTHING!</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411920i/809739.jpg' width='400' height='264' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Fighting for Flight is a sweet and sexy story. An enjoying read that will make your heart clench and sigh with content. Beautiful. And HAWT!<br/><br/><b>Raven</b> Moretti is the victim of her parents lives (I'll certainly come back to that). Raised feeling alone, unloved and unwanted. She lives caged, yearning for freedom, for love, for flight. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411920i/809740.jpg' width='400' height='238' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>A diamond in the rough. A wil</span>
  <span id="freeText3901465538664650649" style="display:none"><b>4 FIGHTING and FLYING Stars<br><br><i>Nothing, not even destiny, could keep me from you.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411920ra/809736.gif" width="500" height="233" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>What does a mechanic...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411920i/809737.png" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>and a fighter have in common?</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411920ra/809738.gif" width="300" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>EVERYTHING!</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411920i/809739.jpg" width="400" height="264" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fighting for Flight is a sweet and sexy story. An enjoying read that will make your heart clench and sigh with content. Beautiful. And HAWT!<br><br><b>Raven</b> Moretti is the victim of her parents lives (I'll certainly come back to that). Raised feeling alone, unloved and unwanted. She lives caged, yearning for freedom, for love, for flight. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411920i/809740.jpg" width="400" height="238" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>A diamond in the rough. A wild flower struggling to survive.<br><br><i>
  <b>“You’re like that single wild flower that grows from the crack in the pavement: miraculous growth with no water source or fertile soil. A person walking by would step around that flower to avoid crushing it. It’s not like the field of wild flowers you tromp through carelessly, crushing them under your feet, knowing that the next day will bring a hundred more.”</b>
</i><br><br>Her path collides with <b>Jonah</b> <i>The Assassin</i> Slade. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411920i/809741._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="327" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>A fighter on the verge of becoming the champion, training for the match of his life. <br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411920ra/809742.gif" width="250" height="184" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote> <br><br>Living unaware, wasting away, until the day he met his saving grace. Raven.<br><br><i>
  <b>“This whole time I thought I was living. But the day I met you, the lights came on. You fill me with things I thought I’d never feel again.”</b>
</i><br><br>To have a life with her, he must sacrifice his dreams, because when a nightmare returns to haunt Raven, he has to decide between the fight and the prize. <br><br>And the prize holds his heart and his happiness in her hands.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401294ra/778742.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>An amazing cast of secondary characters adds spice, depth and feelings in the story.<br><br>Blake, Jonah's best friend and co-fighter, is the most hilarious, awesome and adorable character!<br><br><b>

A prostitute and her diabolical pimp.<br><br>Milena, her mother, does have redeeming qualities and I get that she was scared and abused but woman...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397142ra/766078.gif" width="500" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>What were you doing for 21 freaking years? What kind of idiot decision was that... *bangs head against the wall*<br><br>and then there is:<br><br><b>
  <i>"the DomiDick shit we have to worry about."</i>

I refuse to even use the word father around him...<br>And honestly Dominic:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411920ra/809743.gif" width="400" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><i>Mini-rant ended</i><br><br>This book is definitely worth reading. And <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6888697.Jamie_Salsbury" title="Jamie Salsbury" rel="nofollow noopener">Jamie Salsbury</a> earned a spot in my authors-to-watch-out-for list. My only complaint the use of present tense. I'm not a fan of this technique; it makes a book feel rushed to me, but thank God the story was actually good enough to let that quirk of mine slide.<br><br><b>Blake, you crazy-ass, man-slut I can't wait for your story!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411920i/809744.jpg" width="400" height="256" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548694783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16730934253288524977"><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're my saving grace, Jonah. My angel."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411544i/808616.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Is it possible to find true love in Las Vegas, a city of sins?<br/><br/>A city filled with gamblers and fighters...<br/><br/>A city filled with people with bad intentions...<br/><br/>But at the same time, a city filled with love, hope and good intentions...</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>Raven Morretti --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411544i/808617._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Jonah "The Assassin" Slade --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411544i/808618._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379799427i/654648.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>___________________________________________<br/><br/>When the twenty year old girl <b>Raven Morretti</b> starts working as a mechanic for the famous Vegas celebrity <b>Jonah Slade</b>, she neve</span>
  <span id="freeText16730934253288524977" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're my saving grace, Jonah. My angel."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411544i/808616.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Is it possible to find true love in Las Vegas, a city of sins?<br><br>A city filled with gamblers and fighters...<br><br>A city filled with people with bad intentions...<br><br>But at the same time, a city filled with love, hope and good intentions...</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><b>Raven Morretti --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411544i/808617._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jonah "The Assassin" Slade --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411544i/808618._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379799427i/654648.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>___________________________________________<br><br>When the twenty year old girl <b>Raven Morretti</b> starts working as a mechanic for the famous Vegas celebrity <b>Jonah Slade</b>, she never expected to fall for this tough, UFL fighter. He's a typical bad-boy, known for his many one night stands and the fact that he's NEVER been in a committed relationship. Jonah, on the other hand, never expected this a-typical, yet beautiful girl to get under his skin the way she did, either. The way he sees women is simple: Itch. Scratch. No attachments, no feelings involved. But then, this girl comes sweeping into his world and for the first time in his life, he starts to develop feelings...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Raven is nothing like the girls I'm used to. She's not arrogant or overly aggressive. With her, you get what you see. It's refreshing. I miss her when she's not around. I never miss women. Hell, I go months without seeing my mom and sister. Never bothers me. Raven's been away for twenty-four hours, and I'm going nuts, as if something valuable were missing."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>With a call girl as a mother and the infamous pimp Dominick Morretti (or as Jonah calls him, "Domidick") as a father, Raven has never known what it feels like to be loved and cherished by her parents or any other person close to her. Her parents have neglected her her entire life and she's never had anyone taken care of her. But now that she's met Jonah, she's finally found someone who's willing to fight for her. Someone who's willing to give everything up, just so they can be together. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're a part of me now. I'd do anything for you; I'll fight for your life as I'd fight for my own."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And when Raven's father suddenly shows up with shocking news and an impossible ultimatum, Jonah has to decide just how far he's willing to go to protect his future with the girl he loves so much...<br><br><b>
  <i>Is he willing to fight for love<br><br>Is he willing to fight for freedom?<br><br>Is he willing to Fight for Flight?</i>
</b><br><br>....<br><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411544ra/808619.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Fighting gave me my breath, but you brought me back to life."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411544ra/808620.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Baby, I promise you that you'll never want for physical contact again. I'll always hold you when you're scared" He softly kisses my jaw. "Comfort you when you're sad." His lips brush against my cheeks. "Take care of you when you're sick." Tilting my head back, he kisses my forehead. He bends down and his hazel eyes narrow into mine. "I'll make it my life's mission to make up for every second you were neglected."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/491185.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>Told in a present tense, dual point of view, this story pleasantly surprised me. Granted, because of the many positive reviews, my expectations were quite high and perhaps it didn't fully live up to them, but I still very much enjoyed reading <b>Fighting For Flight</b>. Raven certainly isn't your typical damsel in distress but I did feel sorry for her and for the fact that she had such and awful father (I truly HATED Dominick!!). And Jonah is just your typical, possessive bad boy, but very swoonworhty nonetheless (Okay, I LOVED him!!). <br><br>So, if you're looking for a (a-)typical love story with some very steamy scenes in it, give this one a try!!! And hopefully you'll end up enjoying it as much as I did!!! I'm already looking forward to reading Blake's story in the next part of this series...<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411544i/808621.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"This whole time I thought I was living. But the day I met you, the lights came on. You fill me with things I thought I'd never feel again. You're my angel, baby."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>**4 HIGHLY ENJOYABLE AND FIGHTWORTHY STARS**</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411544i/808622.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>****<br><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_549269425" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/549269425" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/549269425?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cover-lust-i-has-it">cover-lust-i-has-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shy-heroine">shy-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=sports-star-hero">sports-star-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer549269425" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8304048251750852839"><b>Wow!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411626i/808857._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo ravenquote_zpsc07efefb.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There’s really nothing I love more as a blogger than picking up a novel by a relatively unknown author and realising that you’ve struck gold, that the book is going to be a winner. This is just one of those books, the style flows easily, the central characters are easily to believe in and get behind and root for and the story is angsty, tortuous and completely compelling.<br/><br/>This is the story of Jonah and Raven.<br/><br/>Raven is a beautifully drawn character – she’s the daughter of Vegas’ most notorious </span>
  <span id="freeText8304048251750852839" style="display:none"><b>Wow!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411626i/808857._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo ravenquote_zpsc07efefb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There’s really nothing I love more as a blogger than picking up a novel by a relatively unknown author and realising that you’ve struck gold, that the book is going to be a winner. This is just one of those books, the style flows easily, the central characters are easily to believe in and get behind and root for and the story is angsty, tortuous and completely compelling.<br><br>This is the story of Jonah and Raven.<br><br>Raven is a beautifully drawn character – she’s the daughter of Vegas’ most notorious pimp and one of his hookers. Her painful family history and a childhood devoid of love and full of neglect have set her on a path determined to be nothing like her prostitute mother. She’s the polar opposite – a tomboy grease-monkey in coveralls which hide her penchant for expensive lingerie. She’s been dealt a rough hand in life and grew up feeling small and insignificant, crushed by sadness but now she’s making her own way in life, trying to distance herself from her family.<br><br>Jonah has a bad reputation, to put it mildly. He’s a UFL champion fighter and a playboy, sleeping frequently with surgically-enhanced strippers to scratch an itch, as impersonal as you like. He’s dead inside, just moving from one physical encounter to the next. Despite all this, there is a decent guy hidden in there somewhere, he’s from a nice family but his anger over the tragic loss of his father has locked that side of him away.<br><br>The minute he sees Raven for the first time, their eyes lock on each other and the world around them fades away. Raven awakens something inside him and he knows that he just wants to be worthy of her. She’s completely different from the easy women he’s been used to – she has a blatant sex appeal that she seems unaware of and combines it with an almost childlike innocence.<br><br>He knows he wants her with an intensity that shocks him and she stirs a strong protective instinct in him. He feels an all-consuming lust and a life-changing love for her and everything he has worked and fought for is about to be put in jeopardy as Raven’s past catches up with her.<br><br>This is just a beautiful love story. I loved Jonah and his slow re-awakening and his overwhelming love for Raven. It was touching to see how she slowly brought him back to life. Jonah manages to make Raven feel safe, cherished and protected for the very first time in their life but just as they find one another, that happiness is threatened and their love and freedom hang in the balance and the last 15% of the book is a pulsating page-turner.<br><br>This is a great debut novel and is a complete story. There is no cliffhanger and the series will continue with Jonah’s best friend Blake in the next book. Despite it being a full-length novel, I read this very quickly, in one setting – in fact, I devoured it!! It’s a beautiful, compelling romance with a dark, pulsating plot.<br><br>4 stars<br><br>Series Reading Order<br><br>1. Fighting For Flight<br><br>2. Fighting To Forgive<br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i><br></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7508641-amanda-----------?shelf=not-everyone-can-love-you">not-everyone-can-love-you</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer551536995" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9347228798889971329"><br/><br/>This book is for those readers who don’t mind:<br/><br/>1) an insta-love connection<br/>2) insta-lust of the virgin and the one-night-only-casanova<br/>3) buckets of tears from the (stupid) crying heroine<br/>4) overuse of the endearing nicknames of “my girl” and “baby”<br/><br/><br/>This book is <i>not</i> for those who:<br/><br/>1) appreciate character growth and development<br/>2) want a strong, mature, witty heroine<br/>3) enjoy steamy scenes without giggles and crying<br/>4) like to read a believable love story<br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3565108903131923251"><b>4.5 “Assassin” Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsrwbaktfh.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>First things first, I'm sorry I've been way too busy that I didn't have time for you guys. <br/><br/>Seconds, this is what I've been feeling for the past week,<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448410570ra/17135421.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I have over 500 hundred books in my kindle that need to be read and I've been feeling like I have nothing to read. You know what I mean, do you?<br/>When I get like that I usually just start rereading some of my favorite books until something comes along, that is until I realized..<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448410570ra/17135422.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I may be diagnosed with a disease of letting go. T</span>
  <span id="freeText3565108903131923251" style="display:none"><b>4.5 “Assassin” Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsrwbaktfh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448410570i/17135420._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsrwbaktfh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>First things first, I'm sorry I've been way too busy that I didn't have time for you guys. <br><br>Seconds, this is what I've been feeling for the past week,<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448410570ra/17135421.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I have over 500 hundred books in my kindle that need to be read and I've been feeling like I have nothing to read. You know what I mean, do you?<br>When I get like that I usually just start rereading some of my favorite books until something comes along, that is until I realized..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448410570ra/17135422.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I may be diagnosed with a disease of letting go. The number one problem with me is I hold onto something and can't seem to let get. That is what I was doing with my reading. I can't ever just pick up a book for the hell of it. I'm afraid of starting a new book, afraid of the outcome, afraid of the results and if I might like it or not. But isn't that what life is about, taking risks? <br><br>But of course I still couldn't do it. So to make things easier on myself I searched up the books I was gonna reread, which was between <i>Real</i> and <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> (one of my all time favorite books) looked up the similar books and ran across <i>Fighting for Flight</i> and that is how all of this started.<br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br>Jonah is a famous MMA fighter. He is good at what he does. It all started when his father died when he was twelve. His world revolves around fighting, and he is on his way to becoming the next Heavy Weight Champion. His life is simple really, between his family, friends, and fighting it's all he really cares about. He doesn't do relationship and isn't intending to. He is fine with the nameless hook ups.<br><br><b>Ah hell, I don’t even know her name.<br>Oh well. Won’t be the first time I bang a nameless face.</b><br><br>Raven is unlike any other girl. She is a mechanic with a sad past. Her mom is a prostitute and her dad is the biggest criminal in Vegas. She tries to stir clear of her family's history as much as possible. She did a good life for herself between her one BFF and Dog she's satisfied of what she accomplished.<br><br>Jonah came into the shop looking for a mechanic to fix up his classic Impala, Guy of course recommends Raven(the best for the job) and that is how they meet. <br><br>I really enjoyed this book. At first I did feel like the relationship was moving too fast but I over looked it. Of course because of my bae <b>Jonah</b>. He was just the sweetest thing. Totally swooned. <br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsoi0kjxsx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448410570i/17135423._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsoi0kjxsx.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The thing I loved most about this book (besides Blake) was Ravens obsession for VS. I see myself in her. All my money goes straight to VS. that place is my second home. <br><br>Overall, really great book. Glad I read it.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpswe8zwyn5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448410570i/17135424._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpswe8zwyn5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

I Love You :D<br/><br/>This must be the most nail biting book I've ever read!! Jamie Salsbury I will most definately be reading ever other book you EVER write!!! <br/><b>I LOVE BLAKE and CANNOT wait for his book!!! HOTTTTTTTT!!!! </b><br/><br/>I was...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411542ra/808595.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Dominic Moretti a notorious pimp impregnates a beautiful prostitute... But the baby was never hers wasn't it....?<br/><br/>Meet Raven... <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411542i/808596.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A girl who practically grows up alone, with a father who has nothing to</span>
  <span id="freeText5718337174500338487" style="display:none"><b>5 FAN-FUCKIN-TASTIC STARS AND MORE!!! </b><br>Thank you Britney for making me read this!! I Love You :D<br><br>This must be the most nail biting book I've ever read!! Jamie Salsbury I will most definately be reading ever other book you EVER write!!! <br><b>I LOVE BLAKE and CANNOT wait for his book!!! HOTTTTTTTT!!!! </b><br><br>I was...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411542ra/808595.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dominic Moretti a notorious pimp impregnates a beautiful prostitute... But the baby was never hers wasn't it....?<br><br>Meet Raven... <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411542i/808596.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A girl who practically grows up alone, with a father who has nothing to do with her and a mother who doesn't care about her.. A girl who is different, not worried about shopping and money, but someone who is fascinated with cars. Fixing them, building engines.. A girl so innocent, a virgin who is tainted by her parents profession...<br><br>Raven is perfectly content with her life of being alone, her own family is her friends.. She is awesome!! Her cats name is DOG!!!!! soooo cute!!!!<br><br>Then there's Jonah Slade... A Champion fighter.. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379787089i/491322._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jonah brings his car to get fixed at a local mechanic. His told Ray would be fixing it... What Jonah does not know is that Ray is a girl...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411542i/808597.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the moment Jonah meets Raven, it's immediately taken by her.. She's different..<br><br>Life for Jonah is fighting, partying, having sex... With different girls... A man with so many options he never sleeps with the same girl twice. A total man whore and ladies man.<br><br>Raven starts working on Jonah's car at his house.. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411542i/808598.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The more time he spends with her the more he thinks about her... The chemistry is almost instant. <br>Raven has never been touched. Things starts between her and Jonah, she tells him her life.. Her lonely life... He opens to her about secrets he never tells anyone.. She starts staying with him..<br>She tells him she is a virgin... Pure... Jonah is afraid... His afraid that if he sleeps with her, he won't be interested anymore...<br>I think Jonah has ..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411542i/808599.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One day Raven gets a call from her father... She is flabbergasted.. Childhood dreams of her father claiming her and loving her comes to mind.. Raven is hopeful.. Sometimes hope makes us stupid, makes us believe in things which will never happen...<br>Raven goes to meet the famous Dominic..<br><br>I was already in edge at this part...a few OMG moments... Pacing moments... Scared moments... I was finally talked into moving on by my ladies! ;)<br><br>And my WORST fears come true! DAMN!!<br><br>Dominic is coming to claim Raven alright.... JUST NOT THE WAY SHE HOPED!!!!!<br><br>Raven is going to be 21 and breaks it to her that its time for her to be a prostitute just like her mother! If she doesn't, she will kill everyone she loves..... <br><br><b>DREAD</b> filled me.. She finally finds someone and this is what happens???<br>I found myself praying to God that she tells Jonah.. Hahaha!!<br><br>And she does.. Jonah makes a deal with the Devil himself... Dominic wants Jonah to loose the BIGGEST fight of his career. Then he can get her.. <br><br>Easily said than done! Jonah is a champion undefeated.. Will he RISK EVERYTHING for the woman he loves??<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411542i/808600.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At first I was like NO WAY- then I love how the author explains that you can know a person is 'the one' from the time you meet them... <br><br><b> OMG Jonah and Raven have the most steamy loving soul satisfying SEX ever!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411542i/808601.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is some serious panty wetting shit!!     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_547295776" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547295776" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/547295776?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547295776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7175462103743587443"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411333i/807685.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> hmm ok so I know a lot of people are loving this book right now but it just wasn’t quite everything I’d hoped for. </b><br/><br/>Maybe it serves me right for not doing my homework ‘cuz I went into this book blind not knowing anything other than the fact that a lot of people were enjoying it and it had a sexy fighter dude as the hero. That alone sold me on the idea.<br/><br/>It had a strong start. I loved the prologue and the tone it set for the story. I felt both riveted to the story and appalled at what was going on.</span>
  <span id="freeText7175462103743587443" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411333i/807685.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> hmm ok so I know a lot of people are loving this book right now but it just wasn’t quite everything I’d hoped for. </b><br><br>Maybe it serves me right for not doing my homework ‘cuz I went into this book blind not knowing anything other than the fact that a lot of people were enjoying it and it had a sexy fighter dude as the hero. That alone sold me on the idea.<br><br>It had a strong start. I loved the prologue and the tone it set for the story. I felt both riveted to the story and appalled at what was going on. But love the gritty feel of the it and was honestly hooked from there.<br><br>The story is about Raven, the daughter of an infamous Las Vegas pimp who essentially “bred” her (their word, not mine) off of her prostitute mother to literally create the ‘perfect’ hooker for his collection (I’m cringing a little as I write this).<br><br>Jonah “the Assassin” Slade is nearly undefeated in the Octagon and his life as a fighter has treated him well. But he does not do relationships. He does not bring girls home. And he never sleeps with the same one twice. He’s all about the fighting. Its his whole world.<br><br>Until Raven. Seeing her literally changes him and he falls hard and fast for her. But her evil pimp father has plans for her and is not going to let her go easily and soon Jonah finds himself literally fighting for her life.<br><br><i> “You’re a part of me now. I’d do anything for you. I’d fight for your life as I’d fight for my own.” </i><br><br>The writing style varied. I liked it in certain parts and disliked it in others. I felt the dialogue was much too ‘forced’ at times but at other times I found the writing style smart and almost witty. There were several laugh out loud moments and the first part of the story really flew by for me.<br><br>The story started to loose me a little though after the hero and heroine met. I’m very accepting of insta-love but, it has to be handled very carefully and in the case of this story, I just felt it was too much, too soon.<br><br>That being said, I did enjoy part of my read. But there were times when I felt that the story was being told to me rather than allowing me to experience it and the character’s inner monologue of constantly questioning themselves got to me a bit after a while.<br><br><b> I went back and forth between enjoying it and just feeling really disconnected from it. I almost put it down just cuz I really wasn’t ‘feeling’ it but in the end decided to keep going just in case. </b><br><br>I liked Jonah and he had a lot going for him – sexy tattoos and dimples for example – and he was sweet and considerate and VERY protective of her but I had issues with a few of his actions that really made him loose swoon points in my eyes. One was this scene where he pretty much just randomly looses it on her and calls her a ‘bitch’ when seriously, she didn’t do anything deserving of it. *shakes head* SO not cool! And then another thing that rubbed me the wrong way was this: <i> “Fuck. She’s right… The most important thing is to keep Raven calm and safe. That’s where my focus needs to be, at least until this shit is over.” </i> … I’m sorry, I get the whole keep her safe thing, but keep her CALM? Wtf? He was the one with the temper, not her. Ugh.<br><br>I feel like this story could be good. I love the cover, I love the premise and I really liked several parts of the book but over all there were too many things that jumped out at me for me to fully be able to enjoy it. I could see the themes that the author was going for here – feeling worthy of love, feeling appreciated, not judging a person on their background etc but it was the delivery that needed some work. I wanted more time spent fleshing out their relationship, some of the dialogue really needed to be smoothed out and it just needed a bit more… depth to it.<br><br>It wasn’t a bad read though and I know a lot of you have enjoyed it so who knows? Maybe you’ll like it? It just wasn’t really for me.<br><br>Jonah casting:<br><img width="60%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411333i/807686.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="7175462103743587443" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547241668" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10890999303524735938"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411326ra/807671.gif' width='350' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>4.5 stars!<br/><br/>What I loved:<br/><br/>The prologue sucked me in like a vacuum cleaner. <br/>Dual POV---brilliant or superb as my BBF, Anna stated.<br/>Sex scenes---some of the <u>best</u> I have ever read in a NA book.<br/>Loved the characters-<br/>There was not one thing annoying about Raven; she was independent yet young, open and honest, unloved but so lovable. Jonah was all fighter alpha man-whorish. Sweet mama’s boy but bitter over the loss of his Dad when he was young. He never f**ked the same gal twice and had never been in love </span>
  <span id="freeText10890999303524735938" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411326ra/807671.gif" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4.5 stars!<br><br>What I loved:<br><br>The prologue sucked me in like a vacuum cleaner. <br>Dual POV---brilliant or superb as my BBF, Anna stated.<br>Sex scenes---some of the <u>best</u> I have ever read in a NA book.<br>Loved the characters-<br>There was not one thing annoying about Raven; she was independent yet young, open and honest, unloved but so lovable. Jonah was all fighter alpha man-whorish. Sweet mama’s boy but bitter over the loss of his Dad when he was young. He never f**ked the same gal twice and had never been in love until…. he set eyes on his ‘mechanic’- yeah gripe all you want about “insta-love” as this book has it, but I thought it worked. <br><br>There was no bullshit, major misunderstanding, deceit- just in your face open and honest how I feel and I fell in love right along with Raven and Jonah as well as Blake. Loved Jonah’s Mom Katherine as she was completely accepting and supportive of Raven and her checkered past. <br><br>So… some may say “oh how unrealistic” and yeah it is-this is fiction people. But this book is a modern day fairytale that I adored!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“To think that I could experience this all-consuming lust, as well as the soul-shackling love that I would die to keep, is life changing. This tiny girl who works on cars, laughs at stupid jokes, and blushes at the slightest flirtation is mine. There is nothing I wouldn’t do for her. I would spend the rest of my life making her happy if she’d let me. So this is love. My life will never be the same.”-Jonah</blockquote>
</b><br> <br>Fantastic debut novel, Jamie!<br><br><br></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer496001066" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2947858811316062833"><b>*2.5 Stars*<br/><br/>An entertaining read, but fell short of my expectations.</b><br/><br/><i>Fighting For Flight</i> kicked off on a highly intriguing note. I was immediately sucked in to the lives of Raven and Jonah. But as the story progressed, it slowly lost its grip on me and I found myself at a disconnect with the characters.<br/><br/>Raven is your typical gorgeous, insecure, heroine with her v-card still intact—but has suffered an insanely tragic childhood. Her character was endearing, but I felt lacked some personality. Due to </span>
  <span id="freeText2947858811316062833" style="display:none"><b>*2.5 Stars*<br><br>An entertaining read, but fell short of my expectations.</b><br><br><i>Fighting For Flight</i> kicked off on a highly intriguing note. I was immediately sucked in to the lives of Raven and Jonah. But as the story progressed, it slowly lost its grip on me and I found myself at a disconnect with the characters.<br><br>Raven is your typical gorgeous, insecure, heroine with her v-card still intact—but has suffered an insanely tragic childhood. Her character was endearing, but I felt lacked some personality. Due to her uniquely disturbing background, she had the potential of being the most complex, rounded character of the story—and I was disappointed that she never fully rose to the challenge. <br><br>Jonah 'The Assasin', is a UFL fighter who sets aside his infamous playboy ways when he meets Raven. There was definitely an 'insta-love' connection with these two, but it seemed to work fairly well within the story. Jonah was possessive and jealous, but not to an unhealthy extent. He was also very caring and his feelings for Raven felt authentic. Their connection was sizzling hot, and if you enjoy descriptive love scenes, you surely won't be disappointed in that area! <br><br>There were portions of this story that were serious and almost dark, and then there were portions that seemed entirely light and fluffy...giving the overall tone an unsteady feel. I did enjoy the fighting aspect and found myself appreciating it more than the actual romance. Although the ending was somewhat predictable, there were beautiful moments that left me almost teary-eyed. I think this story had potential to fly, but there were a few elements weighing it down. <br><br>All-in-all, a fun and sexy read that I'd recommend to those who love strong, possessive heroes complimented by damaged, innocent, sweet heroines...and, of course, lots of steam! Although it didn't entirely work for me, it seems to be very well received by others—so I hope you all enjoy!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum steam<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Insta-love. Intense, complex, and sexy.<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Alpha, UFL fighter-hero. Sweet, virginal heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Unique and strong concept, Unsteady execution.<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Bold and expressive.<br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Character spinoff (Blake)<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_550163205" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/550163205" />
    <a title="Vishous" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7500821-vishous"><img alt="Vishous" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1424942031p2/7500821.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/550163205?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vishous" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vishous" href="/user/show/7500821-vishous">Vishous</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17449444-fighting-for-flight">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7500821-vishous?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
