        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer550163205" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2260593651574821861"><b>well crud, I wanted to like it a lot but something was just... meh...<br/><br/>I think it was her..</b><br/><br/>With all the good reviews I read I expected something WOW but I just didn't feel that WOW :)<br/><br/>I am giving this book a good solid 3 stars, it would have been 2,5 but I kinda fell in love with side character Blake :)<br/><br/>The book actually started really great for me, I really liked it but I don't know why I kinda lost that feeling. It was pretty predictable from the beginning, and that wasn't even the problem for me.</span>
  <span id="freeText2260593651574821861" style="display:none"><b>well crud, I wanted to like it a lot but something was just... meh...<br /><br />I think it was her..</b><br /><br />With all the good reviews I read I expected something WOW but I just didn't feel that WOW :)<br /><br />I am giving this book a good solid 3 stars, it would have been 2,5 but I kinda fell in love with side character Blake :)<br /><br />The book actually started really great for me, I really liked it but I don't know why I kinda lost that feeling. It was pretty predictable from the beginning, and that wasn't even the problem for me.<br /><br />With <b>Raven</b> being who she is, a mechanic, with actually not so bad past but more like potentially bad future, I expected her to be more stronger, more built up character, yes she has horrible parents but they weren't there, but all I saw was somebody so fragile, on the edge to cry constantly, blinking away tears etc.<br /><br />I kinda expected some cool chick, who doesn't say <i>"crud"</i> or <i>"effing",</i> who doesn't put up with anybody's bullshit but I didn't get that.<br /><br />there's this sentence in this book:<br /><br /><i>"Surviving is nothing to be ashamed of. It's something to be proud of."</i><br /><br />But honestly I felt like everybody else had to do that surviving for her. I wanted her to fought back from the beginning and not accept her bad future, I wanted her to not let Jonah give up on his dreams so she could survive because of him. I wanted her to try and survive by herself with his help, and to show her father that she won't take his bullshit easily.<br /><br />When it comes to <b>Jonah</b> I liked him. I liked him a lot. I can't say he wasn't hot when he was. He wanted to protect her, wanted to have her, to love her, make her his from the moment he saw her, blah, blah, blah... <br /><br />The only thing that got on my nerve was him constantly calling her <i>"my girl, my shy girl, my greedy girl...."</i><br /><br />I really liked their sexy times, it's really not hard to please me with sex in fiction, but the moment when she lost her virginity and was hiding bloody sheets from him and he told her<br /><br /> <i>"i hope it does stain so that every time i sleep on them, i'll be reminded of our first time" </i> <br /><br />I couldn't help myself from picturing him in wrapped bloody sheets, which was a bit turn off that was followed with a burst of laughter. But as all main alpha characters he got my liking again later on.<br /><br />Now the reason for my 3 stars!<br /><br /><b>BLAKE &lt;3</b><br /><br />Now this is a story I seriously can not wait to read! I loved him from the beginning! I loved every cheesy, funny line that got out of his mouth! I wouldn't change a thing about him and I wished he got more time in this book but oh well... he will have plenty of time in his own book :)<br /><br />This story actually had so many potential to be amazing, at least to me, but I guess it didn't live up for my expectations.<br /><br />I can't say I didn't like the story, I did, I just expected something else, more like I expected her to be something that she started to be only at the ending of the book.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>so to sum it up like this:<br /><br />Raven - 1 star<br />Jonah - 4 stars<br />Blake - 5 stars<br />The story - 2.5 stars</b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><br /><b>*buddy read with my gorgeous Shelly*</b></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=everyone-loved-but-duchess">everyone-loved-but-duchess</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-new-adult">genre-new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548692987" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16390399399908792439">A few quick thoughts:<br/><br/><u>
  <b>The good:</b>
</u><br/>*Jonah<br/>*Jonah<br/>*Jonah: The man is amazing...hugely muscled UFL champion, a god in bed, ridiculously tender with his woman and his Mom...nuff said<br/><br/>* Some really skanky adversaries that were actually treated like skanks instead of being sent on their way with a pat on their heads. Maybe I live in a bubble, but does any girl really act this way? Anyhow, they got what was coming to them...<br/><br/>*Blake!!!!! Why do I always fall in love with the oversexed male sidekick? I freak</span>
  <span id="freeText16390399399908792439" style="display:none">A few quick thoughts:<br /><br /><u>
  <b>The good:</b>
</u><br />*Jonah<br />*Jonah<br />*Jonah: The man is amazing...hugely muscled UFL champion, a god in bed, ridiculously tender with his woman and his Mom...nuff said<br /><br />* Some really skanky adversaries that were actually treated like skanks instead of being sent on their way with a pat on their heads. Maybe I live in a bubble, but does any girl really act this way? Anyhow, they got what was coming to them...<br /><br />*Blake!!!!! Why do I always fall in love with the oversexed male sidekick? I freaking LOVED Blake!!! He's unabashedly sexual, and he never lets up...but that's who he is, and it's just accepted. I liked how Raven just laughed him off instead of getting pissed at his chauvinism. It was all in good fun, and he was one of my favorite parts about the book...maybe even more so than Jonah?!<br /><br /><u>
  <b>The bad:</b>
</u><br />* Raven is not the tough chick I thought she'd be. At first, I thought that she was, but soon enough, the tears start to trickle...and flow...and soon I wondered if she'd wash away on her own self made river. She starts to rely on Jonah too much for my tastes. There's one thing about letting a man stand up for you and protect you, but another about hiding behind him and letting him be your shield.<br /><br />* Some of the circumstances seemed pretty fantastical...some of the characters didn't act realistically. One example - why did pimp daddy go to so much trouble to pimp his own daughter? That's like his entire goal since she was a newborn...why? No explanation...there were quite a few sensationalized instances, in my humble opinion. <br /><br />It was still an okay read, but again one that didn't grab me like I wanted it to. <br /><br />A couple of fave quotes:<br />-- <b>"Anyone up for a ride on the bi-polar coaster..."</b><br />(That's Raven speaking of herself...love that she could see her own flaws.)<br /><br />-- <b>"To think that I could experience this all consuming lust, as well as the soul-shackling love that I would die to keep is life changing. This tiny girl who works on cars, laughs at stupid jokes, and blushes at the slightest flirtation is min. There is nothing I wouldn't do for her. I would spend the rest of my life making her happy if she'd let me. <br />So this is love.<br />My life will never be the same..."</b><br /><br />--<b>"That's it!" Locking her eyes with mine, she throws her hands in the air. "I'm done. I'm switching teams. I despise men and from now on will only date women...<br />"Are you going to be okay?" I'm grateful to see her previously purple face fade to a splotchy red.<br />"Me? Hell yeah, I'll be okay. I'm a lesbian now."</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16390399399908792439" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_559809896" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559809896" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559809896?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559809896" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16794034630851609025">I’m doing a re-read via audio version. If you haven’t tried audio, you should do it. It’s the best way to re-read your favorite books or even just try new ones. <br/><br/><b>4 Worth Fighting Stars</b><br/><br/>First off, Fighting for Flight starts out with a BAM and I was instantly drawn into the story. I couldn’t stop reading. JB Salsbury knows how to set-up the story. I felt like it really established the tone and pace for the read. I knew it would be slightly intense and steamy. <br/><br/>Raven doesn’t have the best parents. Her</span>
  <span id="freeText16794034630851609025" style="display:none">I’m doing a re-read via audio version. If you haven’t tried audio, you should do it. It’s the best way to re-read your favorite books or even just try new ones. <br><br><b>4 Worth Fighting Stars</b><br><br>First off, Fighting for Flight starts out with a BAM and I was instantly drawn into the story. I couldn’t stop reading. JB Salsbury knows how to set-up the story. I felt like it really established the tone and pace for the read. I knew it would be slightly intense and steamy. <br><br>Raven doesn’t have the best parents. Her mom is a prostitute and her dad is a famous Las Vegas Pimp. Raven is twenty years old and works a mechanic. I really liked Raven. I found her character unique, sassy and strong. I didn’t know how a Heroine working as a mechanic would work for me, but it completely did. I found it cute reading her gushing over cars.<br><br>Raven is a character and you just feel for. She lives on her own and doesn’t really have friends. Because she doesn’t have the best parents, she’s shy, timid and doesn’t really go out. Jonah has money and is famous. Because Jonah is so high up, women use him for connections and therefore he doesn’t think the best of them.<br><br>Jonah is a famous fighter and has a car he needs restored. Raven goes to Jonah’s house daily to restore his car. Jonah is a player and doesn’t have sex with the same woman twice, but there’s something about Raven that might change his ways. Jonah is SUPER alpha. I love how determined he is. I love that he doesn’t play games and when he sees something he wants he goes for it. He’s apprehensive at first when he meets Raven because he’s never slept with the same woman twice and he’s scared that if he sleeps with Raven then he will lose interest.<br><br>I gobbled up the relationship between Jonah and Raven. I loved how they meet and I love every interaction. Jonah invites Raven to a pool party and Raven doesn’t want to seem needy and Jonah tries desperately to stay away from Raven, but of course everyone is checking Raven out. And it gets Jonah kind of jealous. It’s really adorable.<br><br>The relationship between Raven and Jonah form fairly quickly and I would call it insta-connection. There’s plenty of steam and tension to keep you going. I really liked Jonah’s friends. They are funny and add a little something to the story. We will see more of them in future books. <br><br>More stuff happens and Jonah puts himself in the situation where he has to protect Raven. Yes, I love it too!<br><br>Flight for Flight is about Jonah and Raven’s relationship and the obstacles Raven must face when her past slowly starts to resurface. It’s a dramatic read, with slight tension and a fighting theme. <br><br><b>Audio Questions:</b><br><br><b>Where does Fighting for Flight rank among all the audiobooks you’ve listened to so far?</b><br><br>Fighting for Flight was an easy book to listen to, even though it’s a drama. I could listen to this in one sitting. There’s so much that goes on to keep your interest and there’s plenty of book to listen to. It was well worth the listen. <br><br><b>What other book might you compare Fighting for Flight to and why?</b><br><br>I would compare Fighting for Flight to Vi Keeland’s MMA Fighter series or Katy Evan’s Real series. Both series have a fighter’s theme with strong males and a slightly intense dramatic storyline.<br><br><b>Which character – as performed by Ryan West and Erin Mallon – was your favorite? </b><br><br>I love Erin Mallon. I think she’s one of the best female narrators. I follow her books and I thought she was the perfect Raven. I felt her emotions completely. I also love her voice transitions into other characters, especially the male ones. She does great male transitions. Her voice is light, sweet and unique. <br><br>This is my first Ryan West narration. I love Ryan’s voice. I found it not so deep, but definitely dominate. I could imagine Jonah completely. I thought he conveyed the emotions well and he did great female transitions. I did find his voice a bit slow at times. His pauses were a bit too long for me and so I did speed up his parts by one forth the normal rate. <br><br><b>Did you have an extreme reaction to this book? Did it make you laugh or cry?</b><br><br>I really enjoyed Fighting for Flight. I thought the cover and story was unique. I loved the intro and it was the perfect tone to set for the rest of the book. I was immersed in the story and I felt like I connected to the characters. <br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17167042.Fighting_for_Flight__Fighting___1_" title="Fighting for Flight (Fighting, #1) by J.B. Salsbury" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1357067788s/17167042.jpg" alt="Fighting for Flight (Fighting, #1) by J.B. Salsbury" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00BLADDIY/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00BLADDIY&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16794034630851609025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5226175044318628000">Well if this doesn't define the "everyone loved it but me feeling," I don't know what does. I couldn't get into this and I think the sole reason was Raven. I just couldn't buy into her character. <br/><br/>In my opinion, there's no way the daughter of a drug-prositution ring leader and seasoned prositute-who supposedly continued to work as a prostitute during that daughter's formative years- would end up being like Raven, i.e, a 20 year old virgin mechanic that can't cuss and cries in practically every ch</span>
  <span id="freeText5226175044318628000" style="display:none">Well if this doesn't define the "everyone loved it but me feeling," I don't know what does. I couldn't get into this and I think the sole reason was Raven. I just couldn't buy into her character. <br /><br />In my opinion, there's no way the daughter of a drug-prositution ring leader and seasoned prositute-who supposedly continued to work as a prostitute during that daughter's formative years- would end up being like Raven, i.e, a 20 year old virgin mechanic that can't cuss and cries in practically every chapter. <br /><br />My inability to buy into Raven colored the entire story for me, so I won't get into anything further than that. <br /><br />Anyway, I know everyone else swooned over this one (I wish I had too!) and I'm glad others enjoyed it.     <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer551112095" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6992956721375077678">"I almost lost you."<br/>"No, never. I would've fought. However long it took. I'd never give up until I was free. You're my life, Jonah. My family, my love, my best friend. Nothing, not even destiny, could keep me from you."<br/>He leans forward and brushes his lips against mine.<br/>"Okay."<br/><br/>I must say I really enjoyed this one. Hate wrestling/fighting but said to myself "give it a go". If the prologue doesn't pull you in straight away, I don't know what would. As far as I know it is the first book by this auth</span>
  <span id="freeText6992956721375077678" style="display:none">"I almost lost you."<br />"No, never. I would've fought. However long it took. I'd never give up until I was free. You're my life, Jonah. My family, my love, my best friend. Nothing, not even destiny, could keep me from you."<br />He leans forward and brushes his lips against mine.<br />"Okay."<br /><br />I must say I really enjoyed this one. Hate wrestling/fighting but said to myself "give it a go". If the prologue doesn't pull you in straight away, I don't know what would. As far as I know it is the first book by this author and a job well done. Loved the two main characters. A "true love at first sight" story. When I read that the heroine was only 20, was a bit wary as I like my Heros and Heroines a little older. But Raven had to grow up fast and did not come across as immature and she was working and not in College. Towards the end, during the Big Title Fight and immediately after, my heart was in my mouth. I did not know which way it was going to go .... Jonah fought for this one true love and in the end it all ended Happily Ever After. Not so sure I would be as forgiving of the mother ...<br />Looking forward to the next in this series and the potty-mouthed Blake.<br />Well done to Ms Salsbury for a great book. OKAY!</span>

<div id="review_547634392" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547634392" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/547634392?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=insta-love">insta-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=broken-heroine">broken-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=celebrity-mc">celebrity-mc</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547634392" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer444488200742738815">What do you get when a drop-dead gorgeous tattooed woman named Raven who's an expert mechanic and a bad-ass mixed martial arts fighter meet? The story to end all stories. Oh. My. God. <br/><br/>These two burn up the pages with how much chemistry they ignite. Give me a minute here. *fanning myself…..*<br/><br/>Jonah has never done relationships. He has one use for women and that's purely a one time sexual thing. He has no patience or use for anything more. In fact, just the thought of a woman wanting more has him cr</span>
  <span id="freeText444488200742738815" style="display:none">What do you get when a drop-dead gorgeous tattooed woman named Raven who's an expert mechanic and a bad-ass mixed martial arts fighter meet? The story to end all stories. Oh. My. God. <br><br>These two burn up the pages with how much chemistry they ignite. Give me a minute here. *fanning myself…..*<br><br>Jonah has never done relationships. He has one use for women and that's purely a one time sexual thing. He has no patience or use for anything more. In fact, just the thought of a woman wanting more has him cringing. He's a mixed martial arts fighter and is weeks away from the championship match. This is his only focus. And then he meets Raven. <br><br>Raven is the product of a notorious Las Vegas pimp and one of his prostitutes. You would think that would be the worst of it. You'd be wrong. Her father is a powerful and evil criminal who purposely got her mother pregnant for the sole purpose of breeding an equally beautiful woman to work for him. So on her 21st birthday she will get some pretty bad news. He allows her mother to raise her until this time and she grows up with no love or compassion whatsoever from her. Her mother doesn't want to get attached knowing what her father has in store for her. Despite all the ugliness of her life, Raven emerges as a beautiful, sweet, amazing woman. She has a job as a mechanic and plans to own the shop when her boss retires. What I love about her is that she has so many layers to her. On one side, you see this stunning tattooed woman who works on cars and knows her stuff. So she's probably all hard and tough, (especially with her upbringing) right? Wrong. She's funny, quirky, she doesn't swear and has a heart of gold. Oh, and she's a virgin. Yup.<br><p>
  <i>“You’re like that single wild flower that grows from the crack in the pavement: miraculous growth with no water source or fertile soil. A person walking by would step around that flower to avoid crushing it. It’s not like the field of wild flowers you tromp through carelessly, crushing them under your feet, knowing that the next day will bring a hundred more.”<i></i></i>
</p><p><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411381i/807824.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jonah pulls up to Raven's garage expecting to find a mechanic to help him restore his '61 Impala. He sees Raven "Ray" walk out and he's a goner. The instant attraction is there for both of them and they are tongue-tied and gobsmacked. Jonah invites her to do the work at his house and she agrees. Jonah finds himself thinking and doing things with Raven that are unprecedented. <br>Inviting her to his house? Check. <br>Thinking about her all the time? Check. <br>Fantasizing about her….Check, Check.<br><br>The two of them spend lots of time together working on his car and it's so comfortable and natural right off the bat. <br><br>The secondary characters are pretty great as well. Jonah's fighter friend Blake is hilarious. He's a unashamed horndog and had me cracking up. "If I flip a coin, what are the chances I'll get head?"…somehow he manages to be funny and hot and not pervy. He's actually a sweetheart underneath all that and becomes just as protective of Raven as Jonas. There's one part between Jonas and his mom that killed me…<br></p><p>
  <i>“Mom, I want to tell you I met someone. It’s the mechanic who’s helping me with my car. Things are getting serious between us, and I thought you should know.” Silence. “Mom?” I check to make sure our call didn’t get dropped. Nope, still connected. “Mom, you still there?” She clears her throat. “Yes, Joey, I’m here.” Why is she acting so weird? I know I’ve never had a serious girlfriend before, but I thought she would be off the wall about my finally settling down. “What’s wrong? I thought you’d be excited about my being in a serious relationship.” “Oh, honey, I’m very happy for you. It’s just . . . I guess I thought . . . Well, it’s just a shock, that’s all. I always thought you liked girls.” My eyes bug out of my head and I choke. I cough to clear my voice. “What? Of course, I like girls. Wait, Mom, Raven is a girl! Shit, you thought I was telling you I was dating a guy? Fuck me.” <i></i></i>
</p><p><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/647972.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jonas and Raven connect pretty quickly but they have one huge, massive problem hovering over their heads. Her 21st birthday. Once they become aware of her father's plans for her, Jonah makes a deal with the devil for her freedom. Throw the championship fight and he won't force her into working for him. But things don't exactly go as planned.<br><br>These two are amazing together, the sex between them is off the charts and I was totally in love with their story from page one to end. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411381i/807825._SX540_.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></p><p>
  <i>Everywhere I'm looking now<br> I'm surrounded by your embrace <br>Baby I can see your halo<br> You know you're my saving grace <br>You're everything I need and more <br>It's written all over your face <br>Baby I can feel your halo….<i></i></i>
</p><p>
  <br>
</p></span>

The way he depicted women at the beginning somewhat put me off and affected my estimation of him so the guy has double standards and the worst is that most of the reviewers seem ok with that, glorifying and romanticising the guys treatment towards women and by doing so, they are setting up a very unhealthy agenda that allows men to practice their whoring on women because women are no more than sex object that can be used frequently and any feelings and relationship are forbidden because women only exist for the purpose to satisfy the guys "itch" and "scratch" and the fact of the mater is that this thing is glamorized as if its acceptable in our society for the women to be seen like a piece of meat without a brain! He has the looks, money, fame and can have all the women so why he had sex with the stripper if he can afford all the beautiful women that are panting after him all the time?<br /><br />3. Then he talks about the women's inflated ideas about the romance he said "pretty issues about girl shit," but again, he can screw around girls, to take his itch away and that's absolutely fine with him, but when a women want affection and love it's a "shit." With no equivocation, he did not want any feelings or relationship on any emotional level with a girl, so it seems like he thinks the women cannot and should not have any feelings, romance and wanting an emotional connection, so they are all stupid and ridiculous wanting that with him. Except when he meets Raven, he suddenly wants to have a relationship with her so it is ok for him to have wanted those feelings but not for girls to have them with him?<br /><br />4. I try to push back, clawing my way back to solid ground, when everything in me screams to swan dive off the precipice. </i><br/><br/>Jonah has closed himself off. He refuses to get attached to anyone. He turned his rage into a career as a successful </span>
  <span id="freeText13110534598384395726" style="display:none">They say the eyes are the window to the soul. Raven has her father's eyes. She could not be more different from him. She is the light and he is the dark. She is the hope and he is the harbinger of despair. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><i>I'm balancing on the edge of something huge. I try to push back, clawing my way back to solid ground, when everything in me screams to swan dive off the precipice. </i><br><br>Jonah has closed himself off. He refuses to get attached to anyone. He turned his rage into a career as a successful fighter. He has no idea what to think when he spots a spunky young female mechanic at an auto body shop. She pushes all of his buttons and he immediately feels something. She starts tearing down his walls and she makes him want to protect and cherish her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411632i/808880._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>I've seen you two together:the way he looks at you when you're not looking, like your the sun and he's happily stuck in your orbit. </i><br><br><br>Raven's father has a plan. Raven was meant to be. She has a purpose and he is pushing her toward her destiny. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411632ra/808881.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Raven sees what she could have only to see it all slip away. This tiny girl who works on cars, laughs at stupid jokes, and blushes at the slightest flirtation is mine. I would spend the rest of my life making her happy if she'd let me. </i><br> <br> *****************************************<br><br>This book made me feel so many things. I loved Jonah. He was a hero, a tough guy, a sweetheart and a hot sexy man. He never gave up on what he believed in and he fought for what he believed was right. <br><br>Raven was a strong, independent woman who came into her own. She discovered who she was and what she was meant to be. <br><br>**This is a new favorite for me. I will be looking for this author in the future. **<br><br><b> 5 HUGE STARS</b></span>

<div id="review_610471177" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610471177" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10149843-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593628440p2/10149843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610471177?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/10149843-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610471177" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12843612464169469249"><br/><br/><b> Solid and nail biting 3.5 stars....... </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&current=337f160c1c9a83dc261c3a769f729a88_zpsecc61d39.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420856i/835405._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>'The only daughter of an infamous Las Vegas pimp, Raven Morretti grew up an outsider. Liberated from the neglectful home of her prostitute mother, she finds solace as a mechanic. With few friends, she’s content with the simple life. Flying under the radar is all she knows, and more than she expects.<br/><br/>Until she catches the eye of local celebrity, UFL playboy Jonah Slade. <br/><br/>Weeks away from his title fight, Jonah is determined to stay focused on everything he</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12843612464169469249" style="display:none"><br><br><b> Solid and nail biting 3.5 stars....... </b><br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=337f160c1c9a83dc261c3a769f729a88_zpsecc61d39.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420856i/835405._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>'The only daughter of an infamous Las Vegas pimp, Raven Morretti grew up an outsider. Liberated from the neglectful home of her prostitute mother, she finds solace as a mechanic. With few friends, she’s content with the simple life. Flying under the radar is all she knows, and more than she expects.<br><br>Until she catches the eye of local celebrity, UFL playboy Jonah Slade. <br><br>Weeks away from his title fight, Jonah is determined to stay focused on everything he’s trained so hard to achieve. Undefeated in the octagon, he’s at the height of his career. But resisting Raven’s effortless allure and uncomplicated nature is a fight he can’t win. <br><br>Jonah trades in his bad-boy reputation and puts his heart on the line. But when her father contacts her, setting in motion the ugly truth of her destiny, Jonah must choose. In a high-stakes gamble where love and freedom hang in the balance, a war is waged where the price of losing is a fate worse than death.' </b><br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=840769b787e3e6592359120e3fbb6f91_zps8b986073.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420856i/835406._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Well this was another really entertaining 'tough alpha male meets vulnerable yet strong heroine'. The story in general I loved, there was some great sexual chemistry between Jonah and Raven, and some smokin' hot sex scenes. There was a good deal of romance and some really heart touching moments. There was also an intriguing plot that made me want to keep turning the page and as well as loving the main characters I also loved most of the supporting characters, especially play boy fighter Blake, he really made me smile. (And I'm so flipping happy the next book in the series is about him!!!!)<br><br>So why the 3.5 star rating?, well although there are times that I love a 'quickie' .....this couple went from complete strangers to deeply in love in what felt like a nano second, and although this in no way took away from the excellent and descriptive writing and the engaging and endearing characters, it did make it feel slightly rushed. I would have loved to have been able to see this couples relationship develop at a much more realistic pace, that way we could have really seen what made them tick as individuals and their obviously high sexual chemistry could have grown at a much more believable rate.......rather than the 'Wam, Bam, Thank you Mam' rate.<br><br>Despite this small hitch, I still loved this one, Jamie Salsbury’s debut novel Fighting for Flight is a beautifully written, fighter love story, its definitely worth a read, and I certainly will be on the look out for the next in the series.<br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=b468ebe33f363358b01b538aeb62febd_zps6686030c.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420856i/835407._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12843612464169469249" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText11844012945452177706" style="display:none"><b> ON SALE FOR 0.99 FOR A LIMIT TIME!!! </b> <br /><br /><br /><br /><i> Spoiler free </i><br /><br /><b> “When God hands you a gift, you don’t push it away and tell him ‘later'.” </b><br /><br /><i> This<br /><br /> <br /><br />Book<br /><br /><br /><br />is<br /><br /><br /><br />simply amazing... </i><br /><br /><br />This book is very well written, the characters were captured in their own light that brought them together perfectly. Both POV's was amazing, after each POV I wanted more from that character.<br /><br />I couldn't put this book down for nothing, I was sadly very upset when I was falling asleep from staying up way to late to try to finish this book. I want more from this Author and more of these brilliant characters that holds my heart very deeply. I am ready for Blake. My, my, my, Blake is going to yummy. <br /><br />This book brought out so many emotions in me, I felt anger, hatred, sad, disgusted, happy, laughing my ass off till tears were running out of my eyes, heart warming love that will last a lifetime. <br /><br /><b> Jonah </b> <br /><br />Jonah UFL fighter is drop dead falling to my knees hot as hell. He is a very lovable character. He has so much passion and bring that out in him, very protective that makes me want to hug him and hang from his arm.<br /><br /><b> Raven </b> <br /><br />I absolutely loved her to death.<br /><br /><b> "You laugh even when I'm not trying to be funny. What'd I say?"<br /><br />cover my mouth to muffle my giggles. "You said butt holes." </b> <br /><br /><i> “You’re like that single wild flower that grows from the crack in the pavement: miraculous growth with no water source or fertile soil. A person walking by would step around that flower to avoid crushing it. It’s not like the field of wild flowers you tromp through carelessly, crushing them under your feet, knowing that the next day will bring a hundred more.” </i> <br /><br /><b> You're my saving grace, Jonah.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('n2dPctz0eWRZ8lqnDTAJBJsFHozwKZaBlznEYbchh1uUv0BISIp4ma6T/3FhxSnCHB1L3ntPKr7dwcIyBIpqJg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('T9VAMFwlIlBR+mbO6nBmC1sogD2BTyUZuvg6Wvz5gOhEDU8KyFsjraabwxiGhUbN3DDVbwopmSbwADwJT1JtlQ==')})

  <span id="freeText3044691849074656730" style="display:none">J.B. Salsbury is a New York Times and USA Today bestselling author. She lives in Phoenix, Arizona with her husband and two kids. <br /><br />Her love of good storytelling led her to earn a degree in Media Communications. With her journalistic background, writing has always been at the forefront, and her love of romance propelled her career as an author.<br /><br />She spends the majority of her day behind the computer where a world of battling alphas, budding romance, and impossible obstacles claws away at her subconscious and begs to be released to the page.<br /><br />For more information on<br />her books, or just to say hello, visit JB on her website, Facebook, Twitter, or Instagram. <br /><br />Web: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jbsalsbury.com/">http://www.jbsalsbury.com/</a><br />FB: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/JBSalsburybooks">https://www.facebook.com/JBSalsburybooks</a><br />T: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/JBSalsbury">https://twitter.com/JBSalsbury</a><br />IG: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/jbsalsbury/">https://www.instagram.com/jbsalsbury/</a><br /><br /></span>
